  <span m='1370330'>Semantics</span> <span m='1371080'>is</span> <span m='1371950'>basically</span>
  <span m='1373450'>a</span> <span m='1373510'>branch</span> <span m='1373930'>of</span>
  <span m='1375110'>science</span> <span m='1375700'>of</span> <span m='1376000'>philosophy,</span>
  <span m='1377590'>which</span> <span m='1377800'>is</span> <span m='1377920'>fundamentally</span>
  <span m='1378580'>assigning</span> <span m='1379120'>meaning</span> <span m='1380200'>to</span>
  <span m='1380410'>those</span> <span m='1380650'>objects</span> <span m='1381280'>that</span>
  <span m='1381430'>are</span> <span m='1381500'>described</span> <span m='1381970'>in</span>
  <span m='1382060'>the</span> <span m='1382150'>ontology.</span> <span m='1383380'>And</span>
  <span m='1383500'>so</span> <span m='1384520'>the</span> <span m='1384880'>way</span>
  <span m='1385150'>that</span> <span m='1386080'>we</span> <span m='1386230'>say</span>
  <span m='1386500'>this</span> <span m='1386800'>is</span> <span m='1386980'>that</span>
  <span m='1387210'>it's</span> <span m='1387370'>the</span> <span m='1387490'>relationship</span>
  <span m='1388180'>between</span> <span m='1388870'>the</span> <span m='1388990'>signifiers,</span>
  <span m='1390360'>so</span> <span m='1390490'>the</span> <span m='1390610'>signifiers</span>
  <span m='1391420'>are</span> <span m='1391600'>words,</span> <span m='1392300'>letters,</span>
  <span m='1393250'>symbols,</span> <span m='1394270'>graphical</span> <span m='1394780'>symbols.</span>
  </p><p><span m='1396070'>So</span> <span m='1396250'>how</span> <span m='1396340'>do</span>
  <span m='1396430'>we</span> <span m='1396550'>describe</span> <span m='1397000'>a</span>
  <span m='1397090'>resistor,</span> <span m='1397690'>for</span> <span m='1397840'>example,</span>
  <span m='1398380'>in</span> <span m='1398500'>electrical</span> <span m='1398950'>engineering?</span>
  <span m='1401080'>A</span> <span m='1401170'>squiggly</span> <span m='1401680'>line.</span>
  <span m='1402010'>It's the</span> <span m='1402530'>zigzag</span> <span m='1403060'>line.</span>
  </p><p><span m='1404000'>Well,</span> <span m='1404320'>if</span> <span m='1404500'>you</span>
  <span m='1404560'>don't</span> <span m='1404770'>know</span> <span m='1405100'>electrical</span>
  <span m='1405610'>engineering,</span> <span m='1407140'>you</span> <span m='1407530'>just</span>
  <span m='1407710'>see</span> <span m='1407950'>a</span> <span m='1408010'>squiggly</span>
  <span m='1408490'>line.</span> <span m='1408850'>It's</span> <span m='1409060'>meaningless</span>
  <span m='1409690'>to</span> <span m='1409840'>you.</span> <span m='1410650'>But</span>
  <span m='1410840'>if</span> <span m='1411580'>you</span> <span m='1411700'>know</span>
  <span m='1412030'>that</span> <span m='1412240'>semantically</span> <span m='1413350'>that</span>
  <span m='1413710'>means</span> <span m='1414240'>that's</span> <span m='1414760'>a</span>
  <span m='1414850'>resistor,</span> <span m='1415420'>that's</span> <span m='1415660'>the</span>
  <span m='1415750'>symbol</span> <span m='1416110'>for</span> <span m='1416290'>resistor,</span>
  <span m='1416830'>that's</span> <span m='1417070'>what</span> <span m='1417220'>we</span>
  <span m='1417310'>mean</span> <span m='1417490'>by</span> <span m='1417640'>semantics.</span>
  </p><p><span m='1418930'>And</span> <span m='1419050'>then</span> <span m='1419200'>the</span>
  <span m='1419290'>third</span> <span m='1419650'>is</span> <span m='1419830'>syntax.</span>
  <span m='1421150'>What</span> <span m='1421210'>is</span> <span m='1421300'>syntax?</span>
  <span m='1422090'>It's</span> <span m='1422230'>the</span> <span m='1422350'>set</span>
  <span m='1422560'>of</span> <span m='1422680'>rules,</span> <span m='1423820'>the</span>
  <span m='1424030'>set</span> <span m='1424330'>of</span> <span m='1424750'>principles</span>

  <span m='1430810'>in</span> <span m='1430990'>the</span> <span m='1431230'>ontology</span>
  <span m='1431710'>can</span> <span m='1431920'>be</span> <span m='1432070'>combined</span>
  <span m='1432670'>to</span> <span m='1432820'>build</span> <span m='1433120'>up</span>
  <span m='1433750'>higher</span> <span m='1433990'>level</span> <span m='1434320'>information,</span>
  <span m='1435160'>like</span> <span m='1435580'>sentences,</span> <span m='1436280'>paragraphs,</span>
  <span m='1437710'>and</span> <span m='1438160'>so</span> <span m='1438370'>forth.</span>
  </p><p><span m='1439460'>And</span> <span m='1439510'>so</span> <span m='1439870'>that's</span>
  <span m='1440140'>essentially</span> <span m='1440740'>the</span> <span m='1440830'>construction</span>

  <span m='1443230'>language.</span> <span m='1443770'>So</span> <span m='1443950'>every</span>

  <span m='3853460'>system?</span> <span m='3853790'>And</span> <span m='3853880'>what</span>

  <span m='4437350'>Interface</span> <span m='4437800'>Block</span> <span m='4438040'>Diagram,</span>
  <span m='4438460'>an</span> <span m='4438550'>IBD.</span> <span m='4439110'>And</span>
  <span m='4439510'>this</span> <span m='4439660'>is</span> <span m='4439750'>the</span>
  <span m='4439840'>type</span> <span m='4440080'>of</span> <span m='4440140'>diagram</span>
  <span m='4440500'>that</span> <span m='4440590'>I</span> <span m='4440710'>find</span>
  <span m='4441070'>is</span> <span m='4441160'>really</span> <span m='4441370'>interesting</span>
  <span m='4441760'>representing</span> <span m='4442210'>these</span> <span m='4445240'>interfaces.</span>
  </p><p><span m='4446270'>So</span> <span m='4446370'>here's</span> <span m='4446770'>the</span>
  <span m='4446950'>system</span> <span m='4447220'>engineering</span> <span m='4447610'>ontology</span>
  <span m='4448120'>we</span> <span m='4448240'>typically</span> <span m='4448540'>talk</span>
  <span m='4448780'>about.</span> <span m='4449140'>So</span> <span m='4449770'>this

  <span m='4450550'>of</span> <span m='4450830'>an</span> <span m='4450970'>avionics</span>
  <span m='4451480'>board.</span> <span m='4452200'>So</span> <span m='4452320'>you</span>

  <span m='4453400'>voltage</span> <span m='4453760'>converters.</span> <span m='4454870'>You</span>

  <span m='4456800'>nonvolatile.</span> <span m='4457230'>We</span> <span m='4457660'>have</span>

  <span m='4469580'>SysML,</span> <span m='4469880'>the</span> <span m='4469980'>way</span>
  <span m='4470070'>we</span> <span m='4470160'>talk</span> <span m='4470400'>about</span>

  <span m='4472560'>of</span> <span m='4472620'>the</span> <span m='4472730'>system.</span>
